\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00011}00011 \textcolor{comment}{/* AMD\_2:  performs the AMD ordering on a symmetric sparse matrix A, followed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00012}00012 \textcolor{comment}{ * by a postordering (via depth-\/first search) of the assembly tree using the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00013}00013 \textcolor{comment}{ * AMD\_postorder routine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00014}00014 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00015}00015 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00016}00016 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include "{}\mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h}{amd\_internal.h}}"{}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00023}00023 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00024}00024             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} x ;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00025}00025             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (wflg < 2 || wflg >= wbig)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00026}00026             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00027}00027                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = 0 ; x < n ; x++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00028}00028                \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00029}00029                            \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (W [x] != 0) W [x] = 1 ;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00030}00030                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00031}00031                wflg = 2 ;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00032}00032             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00033}00033             }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00034}00034             \textcolor{comment}{/*  at this point, W [0..n-\/1] < wflg holds */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00035}00035             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (wflg) ;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00043}\mbox{\hyperlink{amd__2_8c_a2a5c31b11d959820a7ed047ccf729a27}{00043}} \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a3de33738fd3c7e77bffbcfaefc3e7645}{GLOBAL}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a84e7b06fe5121a773a03f601eb6b48ee}{AMD\_2}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00046}00046             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} Pe [ ],      \textcolor{comment}{/* Pe [0..n-\/1]: index in Iw of row i on input */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00047}00047             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} Iw [ ],               \textcolor{comment}{/* workspace of size iwlen. Iw [0..pfree-\/1] holds the matrix on input */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00051}00051 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00054}00054             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} Next [ ],                 \textcolor{comment}{/* the output inverse permutation */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00057}00057             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} Elen [ ],                 \textcolor{comment}{/* the size columns of L for each supernode */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00058}00058             \mbox{\hyperlink{amd__internal_8h_a91adff1610bdf681555a8f2e330dc963}{Int}} Degree [ ],}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00063}00063             \mbox{\hyperlink{glbopts_8h_a821030b4c0b76c8ea69c6193548d126b}{abip\_float}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_b_i_p___i_n_f_o}{ABIPInfo}} [ ]   \textcolor{comment}{/* array of size AMD\_INFO */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00064}00064 )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00065}00065 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00066}00066 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00067}00067 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00068}00068 \textcolor{comment}{ * Given a representation of the nonzero pattern of a symmetric matrix, A,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00069}00069 \textcolor{comment}{ * (excluding the diagonal) perform an approximate minimum (UMFPACK/MA38-\/style)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00070}00070 \textcolor{comment}{ * degree ordering to compute a pivot order such that the introduction of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00071}00071 \textcolor{comment}{ * nonzeros (fill-\/in) in the Cholesky factors A = LL' is kept low.  At each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00072}00072 \textcolor{comment}{ * step, the pivot selected is the one with the minimum UMFAPACK/MA38-\/style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00073}00073 \textcolor{comment}{ * upper-\/bound on the external degree.  This routine can optionally perform}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00074}00074 \textcolor{comment}{ * aggresive absorption (as done by MC47B in the Harwell Subroutine}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{ * Library).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{ * The approximate degree algorithm implemented here is the symmetric analog of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{ * the degree update algorithm in MA38 and UMFPACK (the Unsymmetric-\/pattern}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{ * MultiFrontal PACKage, both by Davis and Duff).  The routine is based on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{ * MA27 minimum degree ordering algorithm by Iain Duff and John Reid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{ * This routine is a translation of the original AMDBAR and MC47B routines,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{ * in Fortran, with the following modifications:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{ * (1) dense rows/columns are removed prior to ordering the matrix, and placed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{ *  last in the output order.  The presence of a dense row/column can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{ *  increase the ordering time by up to O(n\string^2), unless they are removed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{ *  prior to ordering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{ * (2) the minimum degree ordering is followed by a postordering (depth-\/first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{ *  search) of the assembly tree.  Note that mass elimination (discussed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{ *  below) combined with the approximate degree update can lead to the mass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{ *  elimination of nodes with lower exact degree than the current pivot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{ *  element.  No additional fill-\/in is caused in the representation of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Schur complement.  The mass-\/eliminated nodes merge with the current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{ *  pivot element.  They are ordered prior to the current pivot element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Because they can have lower exact degree than the current element, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{ *  merger of two or more of these nodes in the current pivot element can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{ *  lead to a single element that is not a "{}fundamental supernode"{}.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{ *  diagonal block can have zeros in it.  Thus, the assembly tree used here}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{ *  is not guaranteed to be the precise supernodal elemination tree (with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{ *  "{}funadmental"{} supernodes), and the postordering performed by this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{ *  routine is not guaranteed to be a precise postordering of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{ *  elimination tree.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{ * (3) input parameters are added, to control aggressive absorption and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{ *  detection of "{}dense"{} rows/columns of A.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{ * (4) additional statistical information is returned, such as the number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{ *  nonzeros in L, and the flop counts for subsequent LDL' and LU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{ *  factorizations.  These are slight upper bounds, because of the mass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{ *  elimination issue discussed above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{ * (5) additional routines are added to interface this routine to MATLAB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{ *  to provide a simple C-\/callable user-\/interface, to check inputs for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{ *  errors, compute the symmetry of the pattern of A and the number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{ *  nonzeros in each row/column of A+A', to compute the pattern of A+A',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{ *  to perform the assembly tree postordering, and to provide debugging}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{ *  ouput.  Many of these functions are also provided by the Fortran}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Harwell Subroutine Library routine MC47A.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{ * (6) both int and SuiteSparse\_long versions are provided.  In the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{ *      descriptions below and integer is and int or SuiteSparse\_long depending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{ *      on which version is being used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{ **********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{ ***** CAUTION:  ARGUMENTS ARE NOT CHECKED FOR ERRORS ON INPUT.  ******}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{ **********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{ ** If you want error checking, a more versatile input format, and a **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{ ** simpler user interface, use amd\_order or amd\_l\_order instead.    **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{ ** This routine is not meant to be user-\/callable.                   **}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{ **********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{ *  method for sparse LU factorization"{}, SIAM J. Matrix Analysis and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Applications, vol. 18, no. 1, pp. 140-\/158.  Discusses UMFPACK / MA38,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{ *  which first introduced the approximate minimum degree used by this}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{ *  [2] Patrick Amestoy, Timothy A. Davis, and Iain S. Duff, "{}An approximate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{ *  minimum degree ordering algorithm,"{} SIAM J. Matrix Analysis and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Applications, vol. 17, no. 4, pp. 886-\/905, 1996.  Discusses AMDBAR and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{ *  MC47B, which are the Fortran versions of this routine.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{ *  [3] Alan George and Joseph Liu, "{}The evolution of the minimum degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{ *  ordering algorithm,"{} SIAM Review, vol. 31, no. 1, pp. 1-\/19, 1989.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{ *  We list below the features mentioned in that paper that this code}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{ *  includes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{ *  mass elimination:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Yes.  MA27 relied on supervariable detection for mass elimination.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{ *  indistinguishable nodes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Yes (we call these "{}supervariables"{}).  This was also in the MA27}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{ *      code -\/ although we modified the method of detecting them (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{ *      previous hash was the true degree, which we no longer keep track}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{ *      of).  A supervariable is a set of rows with identical nonzero}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{ *      pattern.  All variables in a supervariable are eliminated together.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Each supervariable has as its numerical name that of one of its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{ *      variables (its principal variable).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{ *  quotient graph representation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Yes.  We use the term "{}element"{} for the cliques formed during}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{ *      elimination.  This was also in the MA27 code.  The algorithm can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{ *      operate in place, but it will work more efficiently if given some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{ *      "{}elbow room."{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{ *  element absorption:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Yes.  This was also in the MA27 code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{ *  external degree:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Yes.  The MA27 code was based on the true degree.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{ *  incomplete degree update and multiple elimination:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{ *      No.  This was not in MA27, either.  Our method of degree update}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{ *      within MC47B is element-\/based, not variable-\/based.  It is thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{ *      not well-\/suited for use with incomplete degree update or multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00182}00182 \textcolor{comment}{ *      elimination.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00184}00184 \textcolor{comment}{ * Authors, and Copyright (C) 2004 by:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00185}00185 \textcolor{comment}{ * Timothy A. Davis, Patrick Amestoy, Iain S. Duff, John K. Reid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00186}00186 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00187}00187 \textcolor{comment}{ * Acknowledgements: This work (and the UMFPACK package) was supported by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00188}00188 \textcolor{comment}{ * National Science Foundation (ASC-\/9111263, DMS-\/9223088, and CCR-\/0203270).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00189}00189 \textcolor{comment}{ * The UMFPACK/MA38 approximate degree update algorithm, the unsymmetric analog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00190}00190 \textcolor{comment}{ * which forms the basis of AMD, was developed while Tim Davis was supported by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00191}00191 \textcolor{comment}{ * CERFACS (Toulouse, France) in a post-\/doctoral position.  This C version, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{ * the etree postorder, were written while Tim Davis was on sabbatical at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{ * Stanford University and Lawrence Berkeley National Laboratory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{ * INPUT ARGUMENTS (unaltered):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{ * n:  The matrix order.  Restriction:  n >= 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{ * iwlen:  The size of the Iw array.  On input, the matrix is stored in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Iw [0..pfree-\/1].  However, Iw [0..iwlen-\/1] should be slightly larger}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{ *  than what is required to hold the matrix, at least iwlen >= pfree + n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Otherwise, excessive compressions will take place.  The recommended}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{ *  value of iwlen is 1.2 * pfree + n, which is the value used in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{ *  user-\/callable interface to this routine (amd\_order.c).  The algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{ *  will not run at all if iwlen < pfree.  Restriction: iwlen >= pfree + n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Note that this is slightly more restrictive than the actual minimum}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{ *  (iwlen >= pfree), but AMD\_2 will be very slow with no elbow room.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Thus, this routine enforces a bare minimum elbow room of size n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{ * pfree: On input the tail end of the array, Iw [pfree..iwlen-\/1], is empty,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{ *  and the matrix is stored in Iw [0..pfree-\/1].  During execution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{ *  additional data is placed in Iw, and pfree is modified so that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Iw [pfree..iwlen-\/1] is always the unused part of Iw.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{ * Control:  A abip\_float array of size AMD\_CONTROL containing input parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{ *  that affect how the ordering is computed.  If ABIP\_NULL, then default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{ *  settings are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Control [AMD\_DENSE] is used to determine whether or not a given input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{ *  row is "{}dense"{}.  A row is "{}dense"{} if the number of entries in the row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{ *  exceeds Control [AMD\_DENSE] times sqrt (n), except that rows with 16 or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{ *  fewer entries are never considered "{}dense"{}.  To turn off the detection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{ *  of dense rows, set Control [AMD\_DENSE] to a negative number, or to a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{ *  number larger than sqrt (n).  The default value of Control [AMD\_DENSE]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{ *  is AMD\_DEFAULT\_DENSE, which is defined in amd.h as 10.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Control [AMD\_AGGRESSIVE] is used to determine whether or not aggressive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{ *  absorption is to be performed.  If nonzero, then aggressive absorption}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{ *  is performed (this is the default).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{ * INPUT/OUPUT ARGUMENTS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{ * Pe:  An integer array of size n.  On input, Pe [i] is the index in Iw of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the start of row i.  Pe [i] is ignored if row i has no off-\/diagonal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{ *  entries.  Thus Pe [i] must be in the range 0 to pfree-\/1 for non-\/empty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{ *  rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{ *  During execution, it is used for both supervariables and elements:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Principal supervariable i:  index into Iw of the description of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{ *      supervariable i.  A supervariable represents one or more rows of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the matrix with identical nonzero pattern.  In this case,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Pe [i] >= 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Non-\/principal supervariable i:  if i has been absorbed into another}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{ *      supervariable j, then Pe [i] = FLIP (j), where FLIP (j) is defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{ *      as (-\/(j)-\/2).  Row j has the same pattern as row i.  Note that j}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{ *      might later be absorbed into another supervariable j2, in which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{ *      case Pe [i] is still FLIP (j), and Pe [j] = FLIP (j2) which is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{ *      < EMPTY, where EMPTY is defined as (-\/1) in amd\_internal.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Unabsorbed element e:  the index into Iw of the description of element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{ *      e, if e has not yet been absorbed by a subsequent element.  Element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{ *      e is created when the supervariable of the same name is selected as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the pivot.  In this case, Pe [i] >= 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Absorbed element e:  if element e is absorbed into element e2, then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00262}00262 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Pe [e] = FLIP (e2).  This occurs when the pattern of e (which we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00263}00263 \textcolor{comment}{ *      refer to as Le) is found to be a subset of the pattern of e2 (that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{ *      is, Le2).  In this case, Pe [i] < EMPTY.  If element e is "{}null"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{ *      (it has no nonzeros outside its pivot block), then Pe [e] = EMPTY,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00266}00266 \textcolor{comment}{ *      and e is the root of an assembly subtree (or the whole tree if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00267}00267 \textcolor{comment}{ *      there is just one such root).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00268}00268 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00269}00269 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Dense variable i:  if i is "{}dense"{}, then Pe [i] = EMPTY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00270}00270 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00271}00271 \textcolor{comment}{ *  On output, Pe holds the assembly tree/forest, which implicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00272}00272 \textcolor{comment}{ *  represents a pivot order with identical fill-\/in as the actual order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00273}00273 \textcolor{comment}{ *  (via a depth-\/first search of the tree), as follows.  If Nv [i] > 0,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00274}00274 \textcolor{comment}{ *  then i represents a node in the assembly tree, and the parent of i is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00275}00275 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Pe [i], or EMPTY if i is a root.  If Nv [i] = 0, then (i, Pe [i])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00276}00276 \textcolor{comment}{ *  represents an edge in a subtree, the root of which is a node in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00277}00277 \textcolor{comment}{ *  assembly tree.  Note that i refers to a row/column in the original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00278}00278 \textcolor{comment}{ *  matrix, not the permuted matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00279}00279 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00280}00280 \textcolor{comment}{ * ABIPInfo:  A abip\_float array of size AMD\_INFO.  If present, (that is, not ABIP\_NULL),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00281}00281 \textcolor{comment}{ *  then statistics about the ordering are returned in the ABIPInfo array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00282}00282 \textcolor{comment}{ *  See amd.h for a description.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00283}00283 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00284}00284 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00285}00285 \textcolor{comment}{ * INPUT/MODIFIED (undefined on output):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00286}00286 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00287}00287 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00288}00288 \textcolor{comment}{ * Len:  An integer array of size n.  On input, Len [i] holds the number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00289}00289 \textcolor{comment}{ *  entries in row i of the matrix, excluding the diagonal.  The contents}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00290}00290 \textcolor{comment}{ *  of Len are undefined on output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00291}00291 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00292}00292 \textcolor{comment}{ * Iw:  An integer array of size iwlen.  On input, Iw [0..pfree-\/1] holds the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00293}00293 \textcolor{comment}{ *  description of each row i in the matrix.  The matrix must be symmetric,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00294}00294 \textcolor{comment}{ *  and both upper and lower triangular parts must be present.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00295}00295 \textcolor{comment}{ *  diagonal must not be present.  Row i is held as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00296}00296 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00297}00297 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Len [i]:  the length of the row i data structure in the Iw array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00298}00298 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Iw [Pe [i] ... Pe [i] + Len [i] -\/ 1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00299}00299 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the list of column indices for nonzeros in row i (simple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00300}00300 \textcolor{comment}{ *      supervariables), excluding the diagonal.  All supervariables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00301}00301 \textcolor{comment}{ *      start with one row/column each (supervariable i is just row i).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00302}00302 \textcolor{comment}{ *      If Len [i] is zero on input, then Pe [i] is ignored on input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00303}00303 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00304}00304 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Note that the rows need not be in any particular order, and there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00305}00305 \textcolor{comment}{ *      may be empty space between the rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00306}00306 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00307}00307 \textcolor{comment}{ *  During execution, the supervariable i experiences fill-\/in.  This is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00308}00308 \textcolor{comment}{ *  represented by placing in i a list of the elements that cause fill-\/in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00309}00309 \textcolor{comment}{ *  in supervariable i:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00310}00310 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00311}00311 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Len [i]:  the length of supervariable i in the Iw array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00312}00312 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Iw [Pe [i] ... Pe [i] + Elen [i] -\/ 1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00313}00313 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the list of elements that contain i.  This list is kept short}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00314}00314 \textcolor{comment}{ *      by removing absorbed elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00315}00315 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Iw [Pe [i] + Elen [i] ... Pe [i] + Len [i] -\/ 1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00316}00316 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the list of supervariables in i.  This list is kept short by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00317}00317 \textcolor{comment}{ *      removing nonprincipal variables, and any entry j that is also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00318}00318 \textcolor{comment}{ *      contained in at least one of the elements (j in Le) in the list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00319}00319 \textcolor{comment}{ *      for i (e in row i).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00320}00320 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00321}00321 \textcolor{comment}{ *  When supervariable i is selected as pivot, we create an element e of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00322}00322 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the same name (e=i):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00323}00323 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00324}00324 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Len [e]:  the length of element e in the Iw array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00325}00325 \textcolor{comment}{ *      Iw [Pe [e] ... Pe [e] + Len [e] -\/ 1]:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00326}00326 \textcolor{comment}{ *      the list of supervariables in element e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00327}00327 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00328}00328 \textcolor{comment}{ *  An element represents the fill-\/in that occurs when supervariable i is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00329}00329 \textcolor{comment}{ *  selected as pivot (which represents the selection of row i and all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00330}00330 \textcolor{comment}{ *  non-\/principal variables whose principal variable is i).  We use the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00331}00331 \textcolor{comment}{ *  term Le to denote the set of all supervariables in element e.  Absorbed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00332}00332 \textcolor{comment}{ *  supervariables and elements are pruned from these lists when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00333}00333 \textcolor{comment}{ *  computationally convenient.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00334}00334 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00335}00335 \textcolor{comment}{ *  CAUTION:  THE INPUT MATRIX IS OVERWRITTEN DURING COMPUTATION.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00336}00336 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The contents of Iw are undefined on output.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00337}00337 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00338}00338 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00339}00339 \textcolor{comment}{ * OUTPUT (need not be set on input):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00340}00340 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00341}00341 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00342}00342 \textcolor{comment}{ * Nv:  An integer array of size n.  During execution, ABS (Nv [i]) is equal to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00343}00343 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the number of rows that are represented by the principal supervariable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00344}00344 \textcolor{comment}{ *  i.  If i is a nonprincipal or dense variable, then Nv [i] = 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00345}00345 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Initially, Nv [i] = 1 for all i.  Nv [i] < 0 signifies that i is a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00346}00346 \textcolor{comment}{ *  principal variable in the pattern Lme of the current pivot element me.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00347}00347 \textcolor{comment}{ *  After element me is constructed, Nv [i] is set back to a positive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00348}00348 \textcolor{comment}{ *  value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00349}00349 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00350}00350 \textcolor{comment}{ *  On output, Nv [i] holds the number of pivots represented by super}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00351}00351 \textcolor{comment}{ *  row/column i of the original matrix, or Nv [i] = 0 for non-\/principal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00352}00352 \textcolor{comment}{ *  rows/columns.  Note that i refers to a row/column in the original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00353}00353 \textcolor{comment}{ *  matrix, not the permuted matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00354}00354 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00355}00355 \textcolor{comment}{ * Elen:  An integer array of size n.  See the description of Iw above.  At the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00356}00356 \textcolor{comment}{ *  start of execution, Elen [i] is set to zero for all rows i.  During}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00357}00357 \textcolor{comment}{ *  execution, Elen [i] is the number of elements in the list for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00358}00358 \textcolor{comment}{ *  supervariable i.  When e becomes an element, Elen [e] = FLIP (esize) is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00359}00359 \textcolor{comment}{ *  set, where esize is the size of the element (the number of pivots, plus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00360}00360 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the number of nonpivotal entries).  Thus Elen [e] < EMPTY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00361}00361 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Elen (i) = EMPTY set when variable i becomes nonprincipal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00362}00362 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00363}00363 \textcolor{comment}{ *  For variables, Elen (i) >= EMPTY holds until just before the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00364}00364 \textcolor{comment}{ *  postordering and permutation vectors are computed.  For elements,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00365}00365 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Elen [e] < EMPTY holds.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00366}00366 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00367}00367 \textcolor{comment}{ *  On output, Elen [i] is the degree of the row/column in the Cholesky}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00368}00368 \textcolor{comment}{ *  factorization of the permuted matrix, corresponding to the original row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00369}00369 \textcolor{comment}{ *  i, if i is a super row/column.  It is equal to EMPTY if i is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00370}00370 \textcolor{comment}{ *  non-\/principal.  Note that i refers to a row/column in the original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00371}00371 \textcolor{comment}{ *  matrix, not the permuted matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00372}00372 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00373}00373 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Note that the contents of Elen on output differ from the Fortran}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00374}00374 \textcolor{comment}{ *  version (Elen holds the inverse permutation in the Fortran version,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00375}00375 \textcolor{comment}{ *  which is instead returned in the Next array in this C version,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00376}00376 \textcolor{comment}{ *  described below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00377}00377 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00378}00378 \textcolor{comment}{ * Last: In a degree list, Last [i] is the supervariable preceding i, or EMPTY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00379}00379 \textcolor{comment}{ *  if i is the head of the list.  In a hash bucket, Last [i] is the hash}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00380}00380 \textcolor{comment}{ *  key for i.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00381}00381 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00382}00382 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Last [Head [hash]] is also used as the head of a hash bucket if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00383}00383 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Head [hash] contains a degree list (see the description of Head,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00384}00384 \textcolor{comment}{ *  below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00385}00385 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00386}00386 \textcolor{comment}{ *  On output, Last [0..n-\/1] holds the permutation.  That is, if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00387}00387 \textcolor{comment}{ *  i = Last [k], then row i is the kth pivot row (where k ranges from 0 to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00388}00388 \textcolor{comment}{ *  n-\/1).  Row Last [k] of A is the kth row in the permuted matrix, PAP'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00389}00389 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00390}00390 \textcolor{comment}{ * Next: Next [i] is the supervariable following i in a link list, or EMPTY if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00391}00391 \textcolor{comment}{ *  i is the last in the list.  Used for two kinds of lists:  degree lists}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00392}00392 \textcolor{comment}{ *  and hash buckets (a supervariable can be in only one kind of list at a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00393}00393 \textcolor{comment}{ *  time).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00394}00394 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00395}00395 \textcolor{comment}{ *  On output Next [0..n-\/1] holds the inverse permutation.  That is, if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00396}00396 \textcolor{comment}{ *  k = Next [i], then row i is the kth pivot row. Row i of A appears as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00397}00397 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the (Next[i])-\/th row in the permuted matrix, PAP'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00398}00398 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00399}00399 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Note that the contents of Next on output differ from the Fortran}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00400}00400 \textcolor{comment}{ *  version (Next is undefined on output in the Fortran version).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00401}00401 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00402}00402 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00403}00403 \textcolor{comment}{ * LOCAL WORKSPACE (not input or output -\/ used only during execution):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00404}00404 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00405}00405 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00406}00406 \textcolor{comment}{ * Degree:  An integer array of size n.  If i is a supervariable, then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00407}00407 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Degree [i] holds the current approximation of the external degree of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00408}00408 \textcolor{comment}{ *  row i (an upper bound).  The external degree is the number of nonzeros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00409}00409 \textcolor{comment}{ *  in row i, minus ABS (Nv [i]), the diagonal part.  The bound is equal to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00410}00410 \textcolor{comment}{ *  the exact external degree if Elen [i] is less than or equal to two.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00411}00411 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00412}00412 \textcolor{comment}{ *  We also use the term "{}external degree"{} for elements e to refer to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00413}00413 \textcolor{comment}{ *  |Le \(\backslash\) Lme|.  If e is an element, then Degree [e] is |Le|, which is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00414}00414 \textcolor{comment}{ *  degree of the off-\/diagonal part of the element e (not including the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00415}00415 \textcolor{comment}{ *  diagonal part).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00416}00416 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00417}00417 \textcolor{comment}{ * Head:   An integer array of size n.  Head is used for degree lists.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00418}00418 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Head [deg] is the first supervariable in a degree list.  All}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00419}00419 \textcolor{comment}{ *  supervariables i in a degree list Head [deg] have the same approximate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00420}00420 \textcolor{comment}{ *  degree, namely, deg = Degree [i].  If the list Head [deg] is empty then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00421}00421 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Head [deg] = EMPTY.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00422}00422 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00423}00423 \textcolor{comment}{ *  During supervariable detection Head [hash] also serves as a pointer to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00424}00424 \textcolor{comment}{ *  a hash bucket.  If Head [hash] >= 0, there is a degree list of degree}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00425}00425 \textcolor{comment}{ *  hash.  The hash bucket head pointer is Last [Head [hash]].  If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00426}00426 \textcolor{comment}{ *  Head [hash] = EMPTY, then the degree list and hash bucket are both}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00427}00427 \textcolor{comment}{ *  empty.  If Head [hash] < EMPTY, then the degree list is empty, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00428}00428 \textcolor{comment}{ *  FLIP (Head [hash]) is the head of the hash bucket.  After supervariable}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00429}00429 \textcolor{comment}{ *  detection is complete, all hash buckets are empty, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00430}00430 \textcolor{comment}{ *  (Last [Head [hash]] = EMPTY) condition is restored for the non-\/empty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00431}00431 \textcolor{comment}{ *  degree lists.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00432}00432 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00433}00433 \textcolor{comment}{ * W:  An integer array of size n.  The flag array W determines the status of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00434}00434 \textcolor{comment}{ *  elements and variables, and the external degree of elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00435}00435 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00436}00436 \textcolor{comment}{ *  for elements:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00437}00437 \textcolor{comment}{ *      if W [e] = 0, then the element e is absorbed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00438}00438 \textcolor{comment}{ *      if W [e] >= wflg, then W [e] -\/ wflg is the size of the set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00439}00439 \textcolor{comment}{ *      |Le \(\backslash\) Lme|, in terms of nonzeros (the sum of ABS (Nv [i]) for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00440}00440 \textcolor{comment}{ *      each principal variable i that is both in the pattern of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00441}00441 \textcolor{comment}{ *      element e and NOT in the pattern of the current pivot element,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00442}00442 \textcolor{comment}{ *      me).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00443}00443 \textcolor{comment}{ *      if wflg > W [e] > 0, then e is not absorbed and has not yet been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00444}00444 \textcolor{comment}{ *      seen in the scan of the element lists in the computation of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00445}00445 \textcolor{comment}{ *      |Le\(\backslash\)Lme| in Scan 1 below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00446}00446 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00447}00447 \textcolor{comment}{ *  for variables:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00448}00448 \textcolor{comment}{ *      during supervariable detection, if W [j] != wflg then j is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00449}00449 \textcolor{comment}{ *      not in the pattern of variable i.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00450}00450 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00451}00451 \textcolor{comment}{ *  The W array is initialized by setting W [i] = 1 for all i, and by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00452}00452 \textcolor{comment}{ *  setting wflg = 2.  It is reinitialized if wflg becomes too large (to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00453}00453 \textcolor{comment}{ *  ensure that wflg+n does not cause integer overflow).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00454}00454 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00455}00455 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00456}00456 \textcolor{comment}{ * LOCAL INTEGERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00457}00457 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l00458}00458 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01258}01258 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * the current pivot element.  Elen [i] is 1, and there are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01259}01259 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * no variables adjacent to node i.  Absorb i into the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01260}01260 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * current pivot element, me.  Note that if there are two or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01261}01261 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * more mass eliminations, fillin due to mass elimination is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01262}01262 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * possible within the nvpiv-\/by-\/nvpiv pivot block.  It is this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01263}01263 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * step that causes AMD's analysis to be an upper bound.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01264}01264 \textcolor{comment}{                                  *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01265}01265 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * The reason is that the selected pivot has a lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01266}01266 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * approximate degree than the true degree of the two mass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01267}01267 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * eliminated nodes.  There is no edge between the two mass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01268}01268 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * eliminated nodes.  They are merged with the current pivot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01269}01269 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * anyway.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01270}01270 \textcolor{comment}{                                  *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01271}01271 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * No fillin occurs in the Schur complement, in any case,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01272}01272 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * and this effect does not decrease the quality of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01273}01273 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * ordering itself, just the quality of the nonzero and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01274}01274 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * flop count analysis.  It also means that the post-\/ordering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{amd__2_8c_source_l01275}01275 \textcolor{comment}{                                  * is not an exact elimination tree post-\/ordering. */}}
